Breakfast is in another building (Jinxiu Building). You need to go out of the check-in building to another building. Although it is close, it is quite troublesome when it rains. The breakfast is rich in both Chinese and Western flavors, as well as regional specialties. The overall stay experience is very good. I will choose here again next time in Nanning.

Through this incident, I feel that the service is a bit discounted. In addition, if you are in a hurry to go to the airport, it is better not to take the airport bus. The airport bus also runs from the hotel to the train station. After arriving at the train station, you may have to change trains and wait.
